Hooks are a composable extensibility mechanism for extending agent functionality by subscribing to events throughout the agent lifecycle. The hook system enables both built-in components and user code to react to or modify agent behavior through strongly-typed event callbacks.

## Overview

The hooks system is a composable, type-safe system that supports multiple subscribers per event type.

A **Hook Event** is a specific event in the lifecycle that callbacks can be associated with. A **Hook Callback** is a callback function that is invoked when the hook event is emitted.

Hooks enable use cases such as:

-   Monitoring agent execution and tool usage
-   Modifying tool execution behavior
-   Adding validation and error handling
-   Monitoring multi-agent execution flow and node transitions
-   Debugging complex orchestration patterns
-   Implementing custom logging and metrics collection

## Basic Usage

Hook callbacks are registered against specific event types and receive strongly-typed event objects when those events occur during agent execution. Each event carries relevant data for that stage of the agent lifecycle - for example, `BeforeInvocationEvent` includes agent and request details, while `BeforeToolCallEvent` provides tool information and parameters.

### Registering Individual Hook Callbacks

The simplest way to register a hook callback is using the `agent.add_hook()` method:

For multi-agent orchestrators, you can register callbacks for orchestration events:

### Using Plugins for Multiple Hooks

For packaging multiple related hooks together, [Plugins](/docs/user-guide/concepts/plugins/index.md) provide a convenient way to bundle hooks with configuration and tools:

## Hook Event Lifecycle

### Available Events

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;table&gt;&lt;thead&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Event&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Description&lt;/th&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/thead&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AgentInitializedEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered when an agent has been constructed and finished initialization at the end of the agent constructor.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeInvocationEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered at the beginning of a new agent invocation request&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterInvocationEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered at the end of an agent request, regardless of success or failure. Uses reverse callback ordering&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;MessageAddedEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered when a message is added to the agent’s conversation history&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeModelCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered before the model is invoked for inference&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterModelCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered after model invocation completes. Uses reverse callback ordering&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeToolCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered before a tool is invoked&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterToolCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered after tool invocation completes. Uses reverse callback ordering&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;MultiAgentInitializedEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered when multi-agent orchestrator is initialized&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeMultiAgentInvocationEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered before orchestrator execution starts&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterMultiAgentInvocationEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered after orchestrator execution completes. Uses reverse callback ordering&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt; </starlight-tab-item><starlight-tab-item data-label="TypeScript"> &lt;p&gt;All events extend &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;HookableEvent&lt;/code&gt;, making them both streamable via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;agent.stream()&lt;/code&gt; and subscribable via hook callbacks.&lt;/p&gt; &lt;table&gt;&lt;thead&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;th&gt;Event&lt;/th&gt;&lt;th&gt;Description&lt;/th&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/thead&gt;&lt;tbody&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AgentInitializedEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered when an agent has been constructed and finished initialization at the end of the agent constructor.&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeInvocationEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered at the beginning of a new agent invocation request&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterInvocationEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered at the end of an agent request, regardless of success or failure. Uses reverse callback ordering&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;MessageAddedEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered when a message is added to the agent’s conversation history&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeModelCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered before the model is invoked for inference&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterModelCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered after model invocation completes. Uses reverse callback ordering&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;ModelStreamUpdateEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Wraps each transient streaming delta from the model during inference. Access via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;.event&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;ContentBlockEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Wraps a fully assembled content block (TextBlock, ToolUseBlock, ReasoningBlock). Access via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;.contentBlock&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;ModelMessageEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Wraps the complete model message after all blocks are assembled. Access via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;.message&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeToolCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered before a tool is invoked&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterToolCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered after tool invocation completes. Uses reverse callback ordering&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeToolsEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered before tools are executed in a batch&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterToolsEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered after tools are executed in a batch. Uses reverse callback ordering&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;ToolStreamUpdateEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Wraps streaming progress events from tool execution. Access via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;.event&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;ToolResultEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Wraps a completed tool result. Access via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;.result&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AgentResultEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Wraps the final agent result at the end of the invocation. Access via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;.result&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;MultiAgentInitializedEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered when a multi-agent orchestrator has finished initialization&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeMultiAgentInvocationEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered before orchestrator execution starts&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterMultiAgentInvocationEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered after orchestrator execution completes. Uses reverse callback ordering&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeNodeCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered before individual node execution starts&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;NodeStreamUpdateEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Wraps an inner streaming event from a node with the node’s identity. Access via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;.event&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;NodeCancelEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered when a node is cancelled via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeNodeCallEvent.cancel&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterNodeCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered after individual node execution completes. Uses reverse callback ordering&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;NodeResultEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Wraps a completed node result. Access via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;.result&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;MultiAgentHandoffEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Triggered when execution transitions between nodes&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;&lt;td&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;MultiAgentResultEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;td&gt;Wraps the final multi-agent result at the end of orchestration. Access via &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;.result&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;/tbody&gt;&lt;/table&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

## Hook Behaviors

### Event Properties

Most event properties are read-only to prevent unintended modifications. However, certain properties can be modified to influence agent behavior:

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;/docs/api/python/strands.hooks.events/#AfterModelCallEvent&quot;&gt;&amp;lt;code dir=&amp;quot;auto&amp;quot;&amp;gt;AfterModelCallEvent&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;retry&lt;/code&gt; - Request a retry of the model invocation. See &lt;a href=&quot;#model-call-retry&quot;&gt;Model Call Retry&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;/docs/api/python/strands.hooks.events/#BeforeToolCallEvent&quot;&gt;&amp;lt;code dir=&amp;quot;auto&amp;quot;&amp;gt;BeforeToolCallEvent&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;cancel\_tool&lt;/code&gt; - Cancel tool execution with a message. See &lt;a href=&quot;#limit-tool-counts&quot;&gt;Limit Tool Counts&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;selected\_tool&lt;/code&gt; - Replace the tool to be executed. See &lt;a href=&quot;#tool-interception&quot;&gt;Tool Interception&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;tool\_use&lt;/code&gt; - Modify tool parameters before execution. See &lt;a href=&quot;#fixed-tool-arguments&quot;&gt;Fixed Tool Arguments&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;/docs/api/python/strands.hooks.events/#AfterToolCallEvent&quot;&gt;&amp;lt;code dir=&amp;quot;auto&amp;quot;&amp;gt;AfterToolCallEvent&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;result&lt;/code&gt; - Modify the tool result. See &lt;a href=&quot;#result-modification&quot;&gt;Result Modification&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;retry&lt;/code&gt; - Request a retry of the tool invocation. See &lt;a href=&quot;#tool-call-retry&quot;&gt;Tool Call Retry&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;exception&lt;/code&gt; &lt;em&gt;(read-only)&lt;/em&gt; - The original exception if the tool raised one, otherwise &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;None&lt;/code&gt;. See &lt;a href=&quot;#exception-handling&quot;&gt;Exception Handling&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;a href=&quot;/docs/api/python/strands.hooks.events/#AfterInvocationEvent&quot;&gt;&amp;lt;code dir=&amp;quot;auto&amp;quot;&amp;gt;AfterInvocationEvent&amp;lt;/code&amp;gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;resume&lt;/code&gt; - Trigger a follow-up agent invocation with new input. See &lt;a href=&quot;#invocation-resume&quot;&gt;Invocation resume&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; </starlight-tab-item><starlight-tab-item data-label="TypeScript"> &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeToolsEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;cancel&lt;/code&gt; - Cancel all tool calls in a batch with a message. See &lt;a href=&quot;#limit-tool-counts&quot;&gt;Limit Tool Counts&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;BeforeToolCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;cancel&lt;/code&gt; - Cancel tool execution with a message. See &lt;a href=&quot;#limit-tool-counts&quot;&gt;Limit Tool Counts&lt;/a&gt;.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterModelCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;retry&lt;/code&gt; - Request a retry of the model invocation.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt; &lt;p&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;AfterToolCallEvent&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/p&gt; &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;retry&lt;/code&gt; - Request a retry of the tool invocation.&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; &lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

### Callback Ordering

Some events come in pairs, such as Before/After events. The After event callbacks are always called in reverse order from the Before event callbacks to ensure proper cleanup semantics.

## Advanced Usage

### Accessing Invocation State in Hooks

Invocation state provides configuration and context data passed through the agent or orchestrator invocation. This is particularly useful for:

1.  **Custom Objects**: Access database client objects, connection pools, or other Python objects
2.  **Request Context**: Access session IDs, user information, settings, or request-specific data
3.  **Multi-Agent Shared State**: In multi-agent patterns, access state shared across all agents - see [Shared State Across Multi-Agent Patterns](/docs/user-guide/concepts/multi-agent/multi-agent-patterns/index.md#shared-state-across-multi-agent-patterns)
4.  **Custom Parameters**: Pass any additional data that hooks might need

Multi-agent hook events provide access to:

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;source&lt;/strong&gt;: The multi-agent orchestrator instance (for example: Graph/Swarm)&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;node\_id&lt;/strong&gt;: Identifier of the node being executed (for node-level events)&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;invocation\_state&lt;/strong&gt;: Configuration and context data passed through the orchestrator invocation&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; </starlight-tab-item><starlight-tab-item data-label="TypeScript"> &lt;ul&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;orchestrator&lt;/strong&gt;: The multi-agent orchestrator instance (for example: Graph/Swarm)&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;nodeId&lt;/strong&gt;: Identifier of the node being executed (for node-level events)&lt;/li&gt; &lt;li&gt;&lt;strong&gt;state&lt;/strong&gt;: The &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;MultiAgentState&lt;/code&gt; for the current invocation, including an &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;app&lt;/code&gt; field for custom consumer state&lt;/li&gt; &lt;/ul&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

## Best Practices

### Composability

Design hooks to be composable and reusable:

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; ### Event Property Modifications

When modifying event properties, log the changes for debugging and audit purposes:

## Integration with Multi-Agent Systems

Multi-agent hooks complement single-agent hooks. Individual agents within the orchestrator can still have their own hooks, creating a layered monitoring and customization system:

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;AgentLevelHook&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;HookProvider&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;):&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;def&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;register\_hooks&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;(self, registry: HookRegistry) -&amp;gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;None&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; { console.log(\`Agent tool call: ${event.toolUse.name}\`) }) }}// Create agents with individual hooksconst agent1 = new Agent({ id: &#39;agent1&#39;, plugins: \[new AgentLoggingPlugin()\] })const agent2 = new Agent({ id: &#39;agent2&#39;, plugins: \[new AgentLoggingPlugin()\] })// Orchestrator-level hooks via MultiAgentPluginclass OrchestratorLoggingPlugin implements MultiAgentPlugin { readonly name = &#39;orchestrator-logging&#39; initMultiAgent(orchestrator: MultiAgent): void { orchestrator.addHook(BeforeNodeCallEvent, (event) =&gt; { console.log(\`Orchestrator node execution: ${event.nodeId}\`) }) }}// Create orchestrator with multi-agent hooksconst graph = new Graph({ nodes: \[agent1, agent2\], edges: \[\[&#39;agent1&#39;, &#39;agent2&#39;\]\], plugins: \[new OrchestratorLoggingPlugin()\],})&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

This layered approach provides comprehensive observability and control across both individual agent execution and orchestrator-level coordination.

## Cookbook

This section contains practical hook implementations for common use cases.

### Fixed Tool Arguments

Useful for enforcing security policies, maintaining consistency, or overriding agent decisions with system-level requirements. This hook ensures specific tools always use predetermined parameter values regardless of what the agent specifies.

&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;}&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/code&gt;&lt;/pre&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;copy&quot;&gt;&lt;div aria-live=&quot;polite&quot;&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;button title=&quot;Copy to clipboard&quot; ### Limit Tool Counts

Useful for preventing runaway tool usage, implementing rate limiting, or enforcing usage quotas. This hook tracks tool invocations per request and replaces tools with error messages when limits are exceeded.

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; strands &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;import&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; tool&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;from&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; strands.hooks &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;import&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; HookRegistry, HookProvider, BeforeToolCallEvent, BeforeInvocationEvent&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;from&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;from strands import toolfrom strands.hooks import HookRegistry, HookProvider, BeforeToolCallEvent, BeforeInvocationEventfrom threading import Lockclass LimitToolCounts(HookProvider): &amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34;Limits the number of times tools can be called per agent invocation&amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34; def \_\_init\_\_(self, max\_tool\_counts: dict\[str, int\]): &amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34; Initializer. Args: max\_tool\_counts: A dictionary mapping tool names to max call counts for tools. If a tool is not specified in it, the tool can be called as many times as desired &amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34; self.max\_tool\_counts = max\_tool\_counts self.tool\_counts = {} self.\_lock = Lock() def register\_hooks(self, registry: HookRegistry) -&gt; None: registry.add\_callback(BeforeInvocationEvent, self.reset\_counts) registry.add\_callback(BeforeToolCallEvent, self.intercept\_tool) def reset\_counts(self, event: BeforeInvocationEvent) -&gt; None: with self.\_lock: self.tool\_counts = {} def intercept\_tool(self, event: BeforeToolCallEvent) -&gt; None: tool\_name = event.tool\_use\[&amp;#34;name&amp;#34;\] with self.\_lock: max\_tool\_count = self.max\_tool\_counts.get(tool\_name) tool\_count = self.tool\_counts.get(tool\_name, 0) + 1 self.tool\_counts\[tool\_name\] = tool\_count if max\_tool\_count and tool\_count &gt; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;class LimitToolCounts implements Plugin { private maxToolCounts: Record&lt;string, number&gt; private toolCounts: Record&lt;string, number&gt; = {} /\*\* \* Initialize with maximum allowed invocations per tool. \* \* @param maxToolCounts - A dictionary mapping tool names to their maximum \* allowed invocation counts per agent invocation. \*/ constructor(maxToolCounts: Record&lt;string, number&gt;) { this.maxToolCounts = maxToolCounts } name = &#39;limit-tool-counts&#39; initAgent(agent: LocalAgent): void { agent.addHook(BeforeInvocationEvent, () =&gt; this.resetCounts()) agent.addHook(BeforeToolCallEvent, (event) =&gt; this.interceptTool(event)) } private resetCounts(): void { this.toolCounts = {} } private interceptTool(event: BeforeToolCallEvent): void { const toolName = event.toolUse.name const maxToolCount = this.maxToolCounts\[toolName\] const toolCount = (this.toolCounts\[toolName\] ?? 0) + 1 this.toolCounts\[toolName\] = toolCount if (maxToolCount !== undefined &amp;#38;&amp;#38; toolCount &gt; maxToolCount) { event.cancel = \`Tool &#39;${toolName}&#39; has been invoked too many times and is now being throttled. \` + \`DO NOT CALL THIS TOOL ANYMORE\` } }}&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

For example, to limit the `sleep` tool to 3 invocations per invocation:

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;limit\_hook &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;=&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; ### Model Call Retry

Useful for implementing custom retry logic for model invocations. The `AfterModelCallEvent.retry` field allows hooks to request retries based on any criteria—exceptions, response validation, content quality checks, or any custom logic. This example demonstrates retrying on exceptions with exponential backoff:

data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;import asyncioimport loggingfrom strands.hooks import HookProvider, HookRegistry, BeforeInvocationEvent, AfterModelCallEventlogger = logging.getLogger(\_\_name\_\_)class RetryOnServiceUnavailable(HookProvider): &amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34;Retry model calls when ServiceUnavailable errors occur.&amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34; def \_\_init\_\_(self, max\_retries: int = 3): self.max\_retries = max\_retries self.retry\_count = 0 def register\_hooks(self, registry: HookRegistry) -&gt; None: registry.add\_callback(BeforeInvocationEvent, self.reset\_counts) registry.add\_callback(AfterModelCallEvent, self.handle\_retry) def reset\_counts(self, event: BeforeInvocationEvent = None) -&gt; None: self.retry\_count = 0 async def handle\_retry(self, event: AfterModelCallEvent) -&gt; None: if event.exception: if &amp;#34;ServiceUnavailable&amp;#34; in str(event.exception): logger.info(&amp;#34;ServiceUnavailable encountered&amp;#34;) if self.retry\_count &lt; self.max\_retries: logger.info(&amp;#34;Retrying model call&amp;#34;) self.retry\_count += 1 event.retry = True await asyncio.sleep(2 \*\* self.retry\_count) # Exponential backoff else: # Reset counts on successful call self.reset\_counts()&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt; ### Exception Handling

When a tool raises an exception, the agent converts it to an error result and returns it to the model, allowing the model to adjust its approach and retry. This works well for expected errors like validation failures, but for unexpected errors—assertion failures, configuration errors, or bugs—you may want to fail immediately rather than let the model retry futilely. The `exception` property on `AfterToolCallEvent` provides access to the original exception, enabling hooks to inspect error types and selectively propagate those that shouldn’t be retried:

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;class&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;PropagateUnexpectedExceptions&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;(&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;HookProvider&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;):&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#032F62;--1:#9ECBFF&quot;&gt;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;Re-raise unexpected exceptions instead of returning them to the model.&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&amp;quot;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;def&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;def&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;register\_hooks&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;(self, registry: HookRegistry) -&amp;gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;\_check\_exception&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;(self, event: AfterToolCallEvent) -&amp;gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;None&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;:&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;indent&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;if&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; event.exception &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;is&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;// This feature is not yet available in TypeScript SDK&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

### Tool Call Retry

Useful for implementing custom retry logic for tool invocations. The `AfterToolCallEvent.retry` field allows hooks to request that a tool be re-executed—for example, to handle transient errors, timeouts, or flaky external services. When `retry` is set to `True`, the tool executor discards the current result and invokes the tool again with the same `tool_use_id`.

Streaming behavior

When a tool call is retried, intermediate streaming events (`ToolStreamEvent`) from discarded attempts will have already been emitted to callers. Only the final attempt’s `ToolResultEvent` is emitted and added to conversation history. Callers consuming streamed events should be prepared to handle events from discarded attempts.

data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;import loggingfrom strands.hooks import HookProvider, HookRegistry, AfterToolCallEventlogger = logging.getLogger(\_\_name\_\_)class RetryOnToolError(HookProvider): &amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34;Retry tool calls that fail with errors.&amp;#34;&amp;#34;&amp;#34; def \_\_init\_\_(self, max\_retries: int = 1): self.max\_retries = max\_retries self.\_attempt\_counts: dict\[str, int\] = {} def register\_hooks(self, registry: HookRegistry) -&gt; data-copied=&quot;Copied!&quot; data-code=&quot;// This feature is not yet available in TypeScript SDK&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/button&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/figure&gt;&lt;/div&gt; </starlight-tab-item>

### Invocation resume

The `AfterInvocationEvent.resume` property enables a hook to trigger a follow-up agent invocation after the current one completes. When you set `resume` to any valid agent input (a string, content blocks, or messages), the agent automatically re-invokes itself with that input instead of returning to the caller. This starts a full new invocation cycle, including firing `BeforeInvocationEvent`.

This is useful for building autonomous looping patterns where the agent continues processing based on its previous result—for example, re-evaluating after tool execution, injecting additional context, or implementing multi-step workflows within a single call.

Resume input types

The `resume` value accepts any valid `AgentInput`: a string, a list of content blocks, a list of messages, or interrupt responses. When the agent is in an interrupt state, you must provide interrupt responses (not a plain string) to resume correctly.

The following example checks the agent result and triggers one follow-up invocation to ask the model to summarize its work:

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;from&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; strands &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;import&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; Agent&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;from&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; strands.hooks &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;import&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; AfterInvocationEvent&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;resume\_count &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;=&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; You can also use `resume` to chain multiple re-invocations. Make sure to include a termination condition to avoid infinite loops:

#### Handling interrupts with resume

The `resume` property integrates with the [interrupt](/docs/user-guide/concepts/tools/index.md) system. When an agent invocation ends because of an interrupt, a hook can automatically handle the interrupt by resuming with interrupt responses. This avoids returning the interrupt to the caller.

When the agent is in an interrupt state, you must resume with a list of `interruptResponse` objects. Passing a plain string raises a `TypeError`.

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre data-language=&quot;python&quot; dir=&quot;ltr&quot;&gt;&lt;code&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;from&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; strands &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;import&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; Agent, tool&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;from&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; strands.hooks &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;import&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; AfterInvocationEvent, BeforeToolCallEvent&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt; &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;@tool&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;ec-line&quot;&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;code&quot;&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#BF3441;--1:#F97583&quot;&gt;def&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt; &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#6F42C1;--1:#B392F0&quot;&gt;send\_email&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;(to: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;str&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;, body: &lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#005CC5;--1:#79B8FF&quot;&gt;str&lt;/span&gt;&lt;span style=&quot;--0:#24292E;--1:#E1E4E8&quot;&gt;) -&amp;gt; ## HookProvider Protocol

For advanced use cases, you can implement the `HookProvider` protocol to create objects that register multiple callbacks at once. This is useful when building reusable hook collections without the full plugin infrastructure:

<starlight-tab-item data-label="Python"> &lt;div class=&quot;expressive-code&quot;&gt;&lt;figure class=&quot;frame&quot;&gt;&lt;figcaption class=&quot;header&quot;&gt;&lt;/figcaption&gt;&lt;pre 20Z&quot;&gt;&lt;/path&gt;&lt;/svg&gt;TypeScript SDK&lt;/p&gt;&lt;div class=&quot;starlight-aside\_\_content&quot;&gt;&lt;p&gt;The TypeScript SDK does not export a &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;HookProvider&lt;/code&gt; interface. Instead, use the &lt;a href=&quot;/docs/user-guide/concepts/plugins/&quot;&gt;Plugin&lt;/a&gt; class to bundle multiple hooks together. The &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;Plugin&lt;/code&gt; class provides &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;initAgent()&lt;/code&gt; for registering hooks and &lt;code dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;getTools()&lt;/code&gt;
